//////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////// MAIN

int main(void)
{
	Initialization();

	BootScreen();

	auto future = async(StartScreen);
	auto startmusic = async(StartMusic);

	while (!b_check)
	{
		Start();
	}
	if (start == 1)
	{
		HomeStartScreen();
		Sleep(1100);
		b_check = false;
		key = '0';
		auto homemusic = async(HomeMusic);
		Sleep(1200);
		HomeEvent();

	}

	return 0;
}

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

void BootScreen()
{
	SetColor(0, 0);
	BootScreen2();
	Sleep(500);

	SetColor(0, 15);
	BootScreen2();
	Sleep(1500);

	SetColor(3, 7);
	BootScreen2();
	Sleep(1000);

	SetColor(3, 7);
	BootScreen1();
	Sleep(1100);

	SetColor(3, 8);
	BootScreen1();
	Sleep(1200);

	SetColor(9, 8);
	BootScreen1();
	Sleep(1800);

	SetColor(3, 8);
	BootScreen1();
	Sleep(1300);

	SetColor(3, 7);
	BootScreen1();
	Sleep(1200);

	SetColor(3, 7);
	BootScreen2();
	Sleep(1100);

	SetColor(0, 15);
	BootScreen2();
	Sleep(950);

	SetColor(0, 0);
	BootScreen2();
	Sleep(1500);
}

void Start()
{
	StartMenu();
	if (key == (char)LEFT || key == 'a' || key == 'A')
	{
		start = 1;
	}
	else if (key == (char)RIGHT || key == 'd' || key == 'D')
	{
		start = 0;
	}
}

void Initialization()
{
	system("cls");
	system("TITLE 엊첲쟞왤쐑");

	srand(time(NULL));

	system("mode con: cols=75 lines=38");
	system("cls");
}

void StartMusic()
{
	while (!b_check)
	{
		PlaySound(TEXT("Ю.wav"), NULL, SND_ASYNC);
		for (int i = 0; i < 30; i++)
		{
			if (key == (char)SPACE || key == (char)ENTER)
			{
				PlaySound(NULL, NULL, 0);
				b_check = true;
				break;
			}
			std::this_thread::sleep_for(std::chrono::seconds(1));
		}
	}
}

				cout << "뫠모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모뫠" << endl;
				cout << "匣모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모모" << endl;
				cout << "匣匣棨棨棨匣匣匣棨棨棨匣匣匣棨棨棨匣匣匣棨棨棨匣匣匣棨棨棨匣匣匣棨棨棨匣" << endl;
			}
		}
		std::this_thread::sleep_for(std::chrono::seconds(1));
	}
}

void StartMenu()
{
	key = '0';
	key = _getch();

	if (key == (char)SPACE || key == (char)ENTER)
	{
		b_check = true;
	}
}

void HomeEventChoice()
{
	key = '0';
	key = _getch();

	if (key == (char)SPACE || key == (char)ENTER)
	{
		HomeStartScreen();
		HomeChoice();
	}
	else
	{
		HomeEventChoice();
	}
}




//////////////////////////////////////////////////

void HomeChoice()
{
	key = '0';
	key = _getch();

	if (key == (char)SPACE || key == (char)ENTER)
	{
		if (status == 1)
		{
			status = 0;
		}
		if (homecheck == 1)
		{
			fieldcheck = 6;
			b_homecheck = true;
			b_fieldcheck = false;
			FieldHomeScreen();
			Sleep(1300);
			auto fieldmusic = async(FieldMusic);
			FieldChoice();
		}
		else if (homecheck == 2)
		{
			SleepScreen();
			SleepChoiceScreen();
			SleepChoice();
		}
		else if (homecheck == 3)
		{
			UpgradeScreen();
			UpgradeChoiceScreen();
			UpgradeChoice();
		}
		else
		{
			HomeChoice();
		}
	}
	else if (key == (char)UP || key == 'w' || key == 'W')
	{
		if (status == 1)
		{
			status = 0;
		}
		homecheck = 3;
		HomeUpgradeScreen();
		HomeChoice();

	}
	else if (key == (char)DOWN || key == 's' || key == 'S')
	{
		if (status == 1)
		{
			status = 0;
		}
		homecheck = 1;
		HomeFieldScreen();
		HomeChoice();

	}
	else if (key == (char)LEFT || key == 'a' || key == 'A')
	{
		if (status == 1)
		{
			status = 0;
		}
		homecheck = 2;
		HomeSleepScreen();
		HomeChoice();
	}
	else if (key == (char)ESC)
	{
		if (status == 0)
		{
			StatusScreen();
			HomeChoice();
		}
		else if (status == 1)
		{
			if (homecheck == 1)
			{
				status = 0;
				HomeFieldScreen();
				HomeChoice();
			}
			else if (homecheck == 2)
			{
				status = 0;
				HomeSleepScreen();
				HomeChoice();
			}
			else if (homecheck == 3)
			{
				status = 0;
				HomeUpgradeScreen();
				HomeChoice();
			}
			else
			{
				status = 0;
				HomeStartScreen();
				HomeChoice();
			}
		}
	}
	else
	{
		HomeChoice();
	}
}

{
	if (sleepcheck == 0)
	{
		SetColor(13, 15);

		cout << "뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠" << endl;

}

void SleepChoice()
{
	key = '0';
	key = _getch();

	if (key == (char)UP || key == 'w' || key == 'W')
	{
		sleepcheck = 1;
		SleepScreen();
		SleepChoiceScreen();
	}
	else if (key == (char)DOWN || key == 's' || key == 'S')
	{
		sleepcheck = 0;
		SleepScreen();
		SleepChoiceScreen();
	}
	else if (key == (char)SPACE || key == (char)ENTER)
	{
		if (sleepcheck == 0)
		{
			key = '0';
			HomeSleepScreen();
			HomeChoice();
		}
		else if (sleepcheck == 1)
		{
			key = '0';
			sleepcheck = 0;
			b_homecheck = true;
			SleepEvent();
		}
	}
	else
	{
		SleepChoice();
	}
}

void OneCircleError()
{
	system("cls");
	SetColor(9, 15);

	cout << "뫠뫠匣匣匣棨棨棨匣匣匣棨棨棨匣匣匣棨棨棨匣匣匣棨棨棨匣匣匣棨棨棨匣匣匣棨" << endl;	// 1
	cout << "뫠"; SetColor(0, 15); cout << "뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠모모모모모뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠뫠" << endl;	// 2

/////////////////////////////////////////////

void FieldChoice()
{
	key = '0';
	key = _getch();

	if (key == (char)SPACE || key == (char)ENTER)
	{
		if (status == 1)
		{
			status = 0;
		}
		if (fieldcheck == HOME)
		{
			homecheck = 1;
			b_homecheck = false;
			b_fieldcheck = true;
			HomeFieldScreen();
			Sleep(1300);
			auto homemusic = async(HomeMusic);
			HomeChoice();
		}
		else if (fieldcheck == ONECIRCLE)
		{
			if (characterJob == "煎몿")
			{
				OneCircleError();
				DungeonError();
				fieldcheck = 7;
				FieldChoice();
			}

			if (characterLevel > 10)
			{
				OneCircleError();
				DungeonError();
				fieldcheck = 7;
				FieldChoice();
			}
			else
			{
				b_fieldcheck = true;
				
				OneCircleBattleEvent();
				OneCircleBattleScreen();
				BattleChoice();
				Sleep(1300);
				auto dungeonmusic = async(DungeonMusic);

			}
		}
		else if (fieldcheck == 7)
		{
			fieldcheck = ONECIRCLE;
			FieldOneCircleScreen();
			FieldChoice();
		}
		else
		{
			FieldChoice();
		}
	}
	else if (key == (char)UP || key == 'w' || key == 'W')
	{
		if (status == 1)
		{
			status = 0;
		}
		if (fieldcheck == ONECIRCLE)
		{
			fieldcheck = 6;
			FieldHomeScreen();
			FieldChoice();
		}
		if (fieldcheck == TWOCIRCLE)
		{
			fieldcheck = 1;
			FieldOneCircleScreen();
			FieldChoice();
		}
		else if (fieldcheck == THREECIRCLE)
		{
			fieldcheck = 2;
			FieldTwoCircleScreen();
			FieldChoice();
		}
		else if (fieldcheck == FOURCIRCLE)
		{
			fieldcheck = 5;
			FieldFiveCircleScreen();
			FieldChoice();
		}
		else if (fieldcheck == FIVECIRCLE)
		{
			fieldcheck = 6;
			FieldHomeScreen();
			FieldChoice();
		}
		else
		{
			FieldChoice();
		}
	}
	else if (key == (char)DOWN || key == 's' || key == 'S')
	{
		if (status == 1)
		{
			status = 0;
		}
		if (fieldcheck == ONECIRCLE)
		{
			fieldcheck = 2;
			FieldTwoCircleScreen();
			FieldChoice();
		}
		else if (fieldcheck == TWOCIRCLE)
		{
			fieldcheck = 3;
			FieldThreeCircleScreen();
			FieldChoice();
		}
		else if (fieldcheck == FIVECIRCLE)
		{
			fieldcheck = 4;
			FieldFourCircleScreen();
			FieldChoice();
		}
		else if (fieldcheck == HOME)
		{
			fieldcheck = 5;
			FieldFiveCircleScreen();
			FieldChoice();
		}
		else
		{
			FieldChoice();
		}
	}
	else if (key == (char)LEFT || key == 'a' || key == 'A')
	{
		if (status == 1)
		{
			status = 0;
		}
		if (fieldcheck == HOME)
		{
			fieldcheck = 1;
			FieldOneCircleScreen();
			FieldChoice();
		}
		else if (fieldcheck == FOURCIRCLE)
		{
			fieldcheck = 3;
			FieldThreeCircleScreen();
			FieldChoice();
		}
		else if (fieldcheck == FIVECIRCLE)
		{
			fieldcheck = 6;
			FieldHomeScreen();
			FieldChoice();
		}
		else
		{
			FieldChoice();
		}
	}
	else if (key == (char)RIGHT || key == 'd' || key == 'D')
	{
		if (status == 1)
		{
			status = 0;
		}
		if (fieldcheck == ONECIRCLE)
		{
			fieldcheck = 6;
			FieldHomeScreen();
			FieldChoice();
		}
		else if (fieldcheck == TWOCIRCLE)
		{
			fieldcheck = 5;
			FieldFiveCircleScreen();
			FieldChoice();
		}
		else if (fieldcheck == THREECIRCLE)
		{
			fieldcheck = 4;
			FieldFourCircleScreen();
			FieldChoice();
		}
		else if (fieldcheck == HOME)
		{
			fieldcheck = 5;
			FieldFiveCircleScreen();
			FieldChoice();
		}
		else
		{
			FieldChoice();
		}
	}
	else if (key == (char)ESC)
	{
		if (status == 0)
		{
			StatusScreen();
			FieldChoice();
		}
		else if (status == 1)
		{
			if (fieldcheck == 1)
			{
				status = 0;
				FieldOneCircleScreen();
				FieldChoice();
			}
			else if (fieldcheck == 2)
			{
				status = 0;
				FieldTwoCircleScreen();
				FieldChoice();
			}
			else if (fieldcheck == 3)
			{
				status = 0;
				FieldThreeCircleScreen();
				FieldChoice();
			}
			else if (fieldcheck == 4)
			{
				status = 0;
				FieldFourCircleScreen();
				FieldChoice();
			}
			else if (fieldcheck == 5)
			{
				status = 0;
				FieldFiveCircleScreen();
				FieldChoice();
			}
			else if (fieldcheck == 6)
			{
				status = 0;
				FieldHomeScreen();
				FieldChoice();
			}
			else
			{
				status = 0;
				FieldHomeScreen();
				FieldChoice();
			}
		}
	}
	else
	{
		FieldChoice();
	}
}

//////////////////////////////////////////////////

void UpgradeChoice()
{
	key = '0';
	key = _getch();

	if (key == (char)SPACE || key == (char)ENTER)
	{
		if (upgradecheck == 0)
		{
			key = '0';
			HomeUpgradeScreen();
			HomeChoice();
		}
		else if (upgradecheck == 1)
		{
			UpgradeScreen();
			Upgrade2ndChoiceScreen();
			Upgrade2ndChoice();
		}
		else if (upgradecheck == 2)
		{
			UpgradeScreen();
			Upgrade2ndChoiceScreen();
			Upgrade2ndChoice();
		}
	}
	else if (key == (char)UP || key == 'w' || key == 'W')
	{
		if (upgradecheck == 0)
		{
			upgradecheck = 1;
			UpgradeScreen();
			UpgradeChoiceScreen();
			UpgradeChoice();
		}
		else if (upgradecheck == 1)
		{
			upgradecheck = 2;
			UpgradeScreen();
			UpgradeChoiceScreen();
			UpgradeChoice();
		}
		else
		{
			UpgradeChoice();
		}
	}
	else if (key == (char)DOWN || key == 's' || key == 'S')
	{
		if (upgradecheck == 2)
		{
			upgradecheck = 1;
			UpgradeScreen();
			UpgradeChoiceScreen();
			UpgradeChoice();
		}
		else if (upgradecheck == 1)
		{
			upgradecheck = 0;
			UpgradeScreen();
			UpgradeChoiceScreen();
			UpgradeChoice();
		}
		else
		{
			UpgradeChoice();
		}
	}
	else
	{
		UpgradeChoice();
	}
}

//////////////////////////////////////////////////

void Upgrade2ndChoice()
{
	key = '0';
	key = _getch();

	if (key == (char)SPACE || key == (char)ENTER)
	{
		if (upgradecheck == 1 && upgrade2ndcheck == 0)
		{
			key = '0';
			upgradecheck = 0;
			HomeUpgradeScreen();
			HomeChoice();
		}
		else if (upgradecheck == 1 && upgrade2ndcheck == 1)
		{
			key = '0';
			upgradecheck = 0;
			upgrade2ndcheck = 0;

			if (characterJob == "煎몿")
			{
				if (characterMoney >= 100000)
				{
					characterMoney = characterMoney - 100000;

					getjobcheck = 1;
					homecheck = 0;

					b_homecheck = true;
					b_templecheck = false;

					auto getjobscreen = async(GetJobScreen);
					Sleep(1400);
					auto getjobmusic = async(GetJobMusic);
					GetJobChoice();
				}
				else
				{
					UpgradeScreen();
					UpgradeErrorScreen();
					upgradecheck = 0;
					upgrade2ndcheck = 0;
					HomeUpgradeScreen();
					HomeChoice();
				}

			}
			else if ((characterJob == "煎몿" || characterJob == "졺쩤첉" || characterJob == "썖모") && characterLevel >= 41)
			{
				if (characterMoney >= 100000)
				{
					characterMoney = characterMoney - 100000;

					getjobcheck = 1;
					homecheck = 0;

					b_homecheck = true;
					b_templecheck = false;

					auto getjobscreen = async(GetJobScreen);
					Sleep(1400);
					auto getjobmusic = async(GetJobMusic);
					GetJobChoice();
				}
				else
				{
					UpgradeScreen();
					UpgradeErrorScreen();
					upgradecheck = 0;
					upgrade2ndcheck = 0;
					HomeUpgradeScreen();
					HomeChoice();
				}
			}
			else if ((characterJob == "煎몿" || characterJob == "졺쩤첉" || characterJob == "썖모" || characterJob == "쏺죃쌰" || characterJob == "첳촋첉") && characterLevel >= 71)
			{
				if (characterMoney >= 100000)
				{
					characterMoney = characterMoney - 100000;

					getjobcheck = 1;
					homecheck = 0;

					b_homecheck = true;
					b_templecheck = false;

					auto getjobscreen = async(GetJobScreen);
					Sleep(1400);
					auto getjobmusic = async(GetJobMusic);
					GetJobChoice();
				}
				else
				{
					UpgradeScreen();
					UpgradeErrorScreen();
					upgradecheck = 0;
					upgrade2ndcheck = 0;
					HomeUpgradeScreen();
					HomeChoice();
				}
			}
			else
			{
				UpgradeScreen();
				UpgradeError1Screen();
				upgradecheck = 0;
				upgrade2ndcheck = 0;
				HomeUpgradeScreen();
				HomeChoice();
			}
		}
		else if (upgradecheck == 2 && upgrade2ndcheck == 0)
		{
			key = '0';
			upgradecheck = 0;
			HomeUpgradeScreen();
			HomeChoice();
		}
		else if (upgradecheck == 2 && upgrade2ndcheck == 1)
		{
			key = '0';
			upgradecheck = 0;
			upgrade2ndcheck = 0;

			if (characterMoney >= 100000)
			{
				characterMoney = characterMoney - 100000;

				templecheck = 3;
				homecheck = 0;

				b_homecheck = true;
				b_templecheck = false;
				TempleHomeScreen();
				Sleep(1400);
				auto templemusic = async(TempleMusic);
				TempleChoice();
			}
			else
			{
				UpgradeScreen();
				UpgradeErrorScreen();
				upgradecheck = 0;
				upgrade2ndcheck = 0;
				HomeUpgradeScreen();
				HomeChoice();
			}
		}
		else
		{
			Upgrade2ndChoice();
		}
	}
	else if (key == (char)UP || key == 'w' || key == 'W')
	{
		if (upgradecheck == 1 && upgrade2ndcheck == 0)
		{
			upgrade2ndcheck = 1;
			UpgradeScreen();
			Upgrade2ndChoiceScreen();
			Upgrade2ndChoice();
		}
		else if (upgradecheck == 2 && upgrade2ndcheck == 0)
		{
			upgrade2ndcheck = 1;
			UpgradeScreen();
			Upgrade2ndChoiceScreen();
			Upgrade2ndChoice();
		}
		else
		{
			Upgrade2ndChoice();
		}
	}
	else if (key == (char)DOWN || key == 's' || key == 'S')
	{
		if (upgradecheck == 1 && upgrade2ndcheck == 1)
		{
			upgrade2ndcheck = 0;
			UpgradeScreen();
			Upgrade2ndChoiceScreen();
			Upgrade2ndChoice();
		}
		else if (upgradecheck == 2 && upgrade2ndcheck == 1)
		{
			upgrade2ndcheck = 0;
			UpgradeScreen();
			Upgrade2ndChoiceScreen();
			Upgrade2ndChoice();
		}
		else
		{
			Upgrade2ndChoice();
		}
	}
	else
	{
		Upgrade2ndChoice();
	}
}

{
}

//////////////////////////////////////////////////

//////////////////////////////////////////////////

void TempleChoice()
{
	key = '0';
	key = _getch();

	if (key == (char)SPACE || key == (char)ENTER)
	{
		if (status == 1)
		{
			status = 0;
		}
		if (templecheck == 3)
		{
			key = '0';
			templecheck = 0;
			homecheck = 3;
			b_templecheck = true;
			b_homecheck = false;
			HomeUpgradeScreen();
			Sleep(1400);
			auto homemusic = async(HomeMusic);
			HomeChoice();
		}
		else if (templecheck == 1)
		{
			key = '0';
			templecheck = 0;
			seocheck = 1;
			auto seoscreen = async(SeoScreen);
			SeoChoice();
		}
		else if (templecheck == 2)
		{
			key = '0';
			templecheck = 0;
			khancheck = 1;
			auto khanscreen = async(KhanScreen);
			KhanChoice();
		}
		else
		{
			TempleChoice();
		}
	}
	else if (key == (char)UP || key == 'w' || key == 'W')
	{
		if (status == 1)
		{
			status = 0;
		}
		if (templecheck == 2)
		{
			templecheck = 3;
			TempleHomeScreen();
			TempleChoice();
		}
		else if (templecheck == 3)
		{
			templecheck = 1;
			TempleSeoScreen();
			TempleChoice();
		}
		else
		{
			TempleChoice();
		}
	}
	else if (key == (char)DOWN || key == 's' || key == 'S')
	{
		if (status == 1)
		{
			status = 0;
		}
		if (templecheck == 1)
		{
			templecheck = 2;
			TempleKhanScreen();
			TempleChoice();
		}
		else if (templecheck == 3)
		{
			templecheck = 2;
			TempleKhanScreen();
			TempleChoice();
		}
		else
		{
			TempleChoice();
		}
	}
	else if (key == (char)LEFT || key == 'a' || key == 'A')
	{
		if (status == 1)
		{
			status = 0;
		}
		if (templecheck == 1)
		{
			templecheck = 2;
			TempleKhanScreen();
			TempleChoice();
		}
		else if (templecheck == 2)
		{
			templecheck = 1;
			TempleSeoScreen();
			TempleChoice();
		}
		else if (templecheck == 3)
		{
			templecheck = 1;
			TempleSeoScreen();
			TempleChoice();
		}
		else
		{
			TempleChoice();
		}
	}
	else if (key == (char)RIGHT || key == 'd' || key == 'D')
	{
		if (status == 1)
		{
			status = 0;
		}
		if (templecheck == 1 || templecheck == 2)
		{
			templecheck = 3;
			TempleHomeScreen();
			TempleChoice();
		}
		else
		{
			TempleChoice();
		}
	}
	else if (key == (char)ESC)
	{
		if (status == 0)
		{
			StatusScreen();
			TempleChoice();
		}
		else if (status == 1)
		{
			if (templecheck = 1)
			{
				status = 0;
				TempleSeoScreen();
				TempleChoice();
			}
			else if (templecheck = 2)
			{
				status = 0;
				TempleKhanScreen();
				TempleChoice();
			}
			else if (templecheck = 3)
			{
				status = 0;
				TempleHomeScreen();
				TempleChoice();
			}
			else
			{
				status = 0;
				TempleHomeScreen();
				TempleChoice();
			}
		}
	}
	else
	{
		TempleChoice();
	}
}



//////////////////////////////////////////////////

void SeoScreen()
{

	for (int i = 0; i >= 0; i++)
	{
		if (seocheck == 0)
		{
			i = -2;
		}
		else if (seocheck == 1)
		{
			system("cls");
			SetColor(9, 15);

//////////////////////////////////////////////////

void GetJobChoice()
{
	key = '0';
	key = _getch();

	if (key == (char)SPACE || key == (char)ENTER)
	{
		if (getjobcheck == 1)
		{
			key = '0';
			getjobcheck = 0;
			homecheck = 3;
			b_getjobcheck = true;
			b_homecheck = false;
			HomeUpgradeScreen();
			Sleep(1400);
			auto homemusic = async(HomeMusic);
			HomeChoice();
		}
		else if (getjobcheck == 2)
		{
			if (characterJob == "煎몿")
			{
				getjobcheck = 3;
				GetJobChoice();
			}
			else if (characterJob == "졺쩤첉" || characterJob == "썖모" || characterJob == "쏺죃쌰" || characterJob == "첳촋첉")
			{
				getjobcheck = 13;
				GetJobChoice();
			}
			else
			{
				getjobcheck = 27;
				GetJobChoice();
			}
		}
		else if (getjobcheck == 3)
		{
			getjobcheck = 2;
			GetJobChoice();
		}
		else if (getjobcheck == 4)
		{
			getjobcheck = 5;
			GetJobChoice();
		}
		else if (getjobcheck == 5)
		{
			getjobcheck = 7;
			GetJobChoice();
		}
		else if (getjobcheck == 6)
		{
			getjobcheck = 10;
			GetJobChoice();
		}
		else if (getjobcheck == 8)
		{
			getjobcheck = 9;
			characterJob = "썖모";
			characterSkill1 = "얾콪썧";
			GetJobChoice();
		}
		else if (getjobcheck == 11)
		{
			getjobcheck = 12;
			characterJob = "졺쩤첉";
			characterSkill1 = "쥠胄";
			GetJobChoice();
		}
		else if (getjobcheck == 14)
		{
			if (characterJob == "졺쩤첉" && characterLevel >= 41)
			{
				getjobcheck = 15;
				GetJobChoice();
			}
			else if (characterJob == "썖모" && characterLevel >= 41)
			{
				getjobcheck = 18;
				GetJobChoice();
			}
			else if (characterJob == "쏺죃쌰" && characterLevel >= 71)
			{
				getjobcheck = 21;
				GetJobChoice();
			}
			else if (characterJob == "첳촋첉" && characterLevel >= 71)
			{
				getjobcheck = 24;
				GetJobChoice();
			}
			else
			{
				getjobcheck = 27;
				GetJobChoice();
			}
		}
		else if (getjobcheck == 16)
		{
			getjobcheck = 17;
			characterJob = "쏺죃쌰";
			characterSkill2 = "큊첲";
			GetJobChoice();
		}
		else if (getjobcheck == 19)
		{
			getjobcheck = 20;
			characterJob = "첳촋첉";
			characterSkill2 = "좰첉첊쨨";
			GetJobChoice();
		}
		else if (getjobcheck == 22)
		{
			getjobcheck = 23;
			characterJob = "턄썭첉";
			characterSkill3 = "쏛퀛츂";
			GetJobChoice();
		}
		else if (getjobcheck == 25)
		{
			getjobcheck = 26;
			characterJob = "첳촋";
			characterSkill3 = "컫쵖썧";
			GetJobChoice();
		}
		else if (getjobcheck == 7 || getjobcheck == 9 || getjobcheck == 10 || getjobcheck == 12 || getjobcheck == 13 || getjobcheck == 15 || getjobcheck == 17 || getjobcheck == 18 || getjobcheck == 20 || getjobcheck == 21 || getjobcheck == 23 || getjobcheck == 24 || getjobcheck == 26 || getjobcheck == 27)
		{
			getjobcheck = 2;
			GetJobChoice();
		}
		else
		{
			GetJobChoice();
		}
	}
	else if (key == (char)LEFT || key == 'a' || key == 'A')
	{
		if (getjobcheck == 1)
		{
			getjobcheck = 2;
			GetJobChoice();
		}
		else
		{
			GetJobChoice();
		}
	}
	else if (key == (char)RIGHT || key == 'd' || key == 'D')
	{
		if (getjobcheck == 2)
		{
			getjobcheck = 1;
			GetJobChoice();
		}
		else
		{
			GetJobChoice();
		}
	}
	else if (key == (char)UP || key == 'w' || key == 'W')
	{
		if (getjobcheck == 3)
		{
			getjobcheck = 4;
			GetJobChoice();
		}
		else if (getjobcheck == 5)
		{
			getjobcheck = 6;
			GetJobChoice();
		}
		else if (getjobcheck == 7)
		{
			getjobcheck = 8;
			GetJobChoice();
		}
		else if (getjobcheck == 10)
		{
			getjobcheck = 11;
			GetJobChoice();
		}
		else if (getjobcheck == 13)
		{
			getjobcheck = 14;
			GetJobChoice();
		}
		else if (getjobcheck == 15)
		{
			getjobcheck = 16;
			GetJobChoice();
		}
		else if (getjobcheck == 18)
		{
			getjobcheck = 19;
			GetJobChoice();
		}
		else if (getjobcheck == 21)
		{
			getjobcheck = 22;
			GetJobChoice();
		}
		else if (getjobcheck == 24)
		{
			getjobcheck = 25;
			GetJobChoice();
		}
		else
		{
			GetJobChoice();
		}
	}
	else if (key == (char)DOWN || key == 's' || key == 'S')
	{
		if (getjobcheck == 4)
		{
			getjobcheck = 3;
			GetJobChoice();
		}
		else if (getjobcheck == 6)
		{
			getjobcheck = 5;
			GetJobChoice();
		}
		else if (getjobcheck == 8)
		{
			getjobcheck = 7;
			GetJobChoice();
		}
		else if (getjobcheck == 11)
		{
			getjobcheck = 10;
			GetJobChoice();
		}
		else if (getjobcheck == 14)
		{
			getjobcheck = 13;
			GetJobChoice();
		}
		else if (getjobcheck == 16)
		{
			getjobcheck = 15;
			GetJobChoice();
		}
		else if (getjobcheck == 19)
		{
			getjobcheck = 18;
			GetJobChoice();
		}
		else if (getjobcheck == 22)
		{
			getjobcheck = 21;
			GetJobChoice();
		}
		else if (getjobcheck == 25)
		{
			getjobcheck = 24;
			GetJobChoice();
		}
		else
		{
			GetJobChoice();
		}
	}
	else
	{
		GetJobChoice();
	}
}

{

	for (int i = 0; i >= 0; i++)
	{
		if (khancheck == 0)
		{
			i = -2;
		}
		else if (khancheck == 1)
		{
			system("cls");
			SetColor(9, 15);

			cout << "뫠뫠匣匣匣棨棨棨匣匣匣棨棨棨匣匣匣棨棨棨匣匣匣棨棨棨匣匣匣棨棨棨匣匣匣棨" << endl;	// 1

//////////////////////////////////////////////////

void SeoChoice()
{
	key = '0';
	key = _getch();

	if (key == (char)SPACE || key == (char)ENTER)
	{
		if (seocheck == 1)
		{
			seocheck = 0;
			templecheck = 1;
			Sleep(1200);
			TempleSeoScreen();
			TempleChoice();
		}
		else if (seocheck == 2)
		{
			seocheck = 3;
			SeoChoice();
		}
		else if (seocheck == 3)
		{
			seocheck = 5;
			SeoChoice();
		}
		else if (seocheck == 4)
		{
			seocheck = 6;
			SeoChoice();
		}
		else if (seocheck == 5)
		{
			seocheck = 2;
			SeoChoice();
		}
		else if (seocheck == 6)
		{
			seocheck = 2;
			SeoChoice();
		}
		else if (seocheck == 7)
		{
			if (characterMoney >= 150000)
			{
				characterMoney = characterMoney - 150000;
				characterMaxHp = characterMaxHp + 500;
				seocheck = 8;
				SeoChoice();
			}
			else
			{
				seocheck = 9;
				SeoChoice();
			}
		}
		else if (seocheck == 8)
		{
			seocheck = 2;
			SeoChoice();
		}
		else if (seocheck == 9)
		{
			seocheck = 2;
			SeoChoice();
		}
		else
		{
			SeoChoice();
		}
	}
	else if (key == (char)LEFT || key == 'a' || key == 'A')
	{
		if (seocheck == 1)
		{
			seocheck = 2;
			SeoChoice();
		}
		else
		{
			SeoChoice();
		}
	}
	else if (key == (char)RIGHT || key == 'd' || key == 'D')
	{
		if (seocheck == 2)
		{
			seocheck = 1;
			SeoChoice();
		}
		else
		{
			SeoChoice();
		}
	}
	else if (key == (char)UP || key == 'w' || key == 'W')
	{
		if (seocheck == 3)
		{
			seocheck = 4;
			SeoChoice();
		}
		else if (seocheck == 6)
		{
			seocheck = 7;
			SeoChoice();
		}
		else
		{
			SeoChoice();
		}
	}
	else if (key == (char)DOWN || key == 's' || key == 'S')
	{
		if (seocheck == 4)
		{
			seocheck = 3;
			SeoChoice();
		}
		else if (seocheck == 7)
		{
			seocheck = 6;
			SeoChoice();
		}
		else
		{
			SeoChoice();
		}
	}
	else
	{
		SeoChoice();
	}
}

//////////////////////////////////////////////////

void HomeMusic()
{
	while (!b_homecheck)
	{
		PlaySound(TEXT("쵛.wav"), NULL, SND_ASYNC);
		for (int i = 0; i < 48; i++)
		{
			if (homecheck == 1 && (key == (char)SPACE || key == (char)ENTER))
			{
				PlaySound(NULL, NULL, 0);
				b_homecheck = true;
				break;
			}
			else if (b_homecheck == true)
			{
				PlaySound(NULL, NULL, 0);
				break;
			}
			std::this_thread::sleep_for(std::chrono::seconds(1));
		}
	}
	b_homecheck = false;
	homecheck = 0;
}

//////////////////////////////////////////////////

void FieldMusic()
{

	while (!b_fieldcheck)
	{
		PlaySound(TEXT("퉛.wav"), NULL, SND_ASYNC);
		for (int i = 0; i < 59; i++)
		{
			if (fieldcheck == 6 && (key == (char)SPACE || key == (char)ENTER))
			{
				key = '0';
				PlaySound(NULL, NULL, 0);
				b_fieldcheck = true;
				break;
			}
			else if (fieldcheck == 1 && (key == (char)SPACE || key == (char)ENTER))
			{
				key = '0';
				PlaySound(NULL, NULL, 0);
				b_fieldcheck = true;
				break;
			}
			else if (b_fieldcheck == true)
			{
				PlaySound(NULL, NULL, 0);
				break;
			}
			std::this_thread::sleep_for(std::chrono::seconds(1));
		}
	}
	b_fieldcheck = false;
	fieldcheck = 0;
}

void DungeonMusic()
{
	while (!b_dungeoncheck)
	{
		PlaySound(TEXT("첲쾟.wav"), NULL, SND_ASYNC);
		for (int i = 0; i < 68; i++)
		{
			if (b_dungeoncheck == true)
			{
				key = '0';
				PlaySound(NULL, NULL, 0);
				break;
			}
			std::this_thread::sleep_for(std::chrono::seconds(1));
		}
	}
	b_dungeoncheck = false;
}


//////////////////////////////////////////////////

//////////////////////////////////////////////////

void SetColor(int color, int bgcolor)
{
	bgcolor &= 0xf;
	color &= 0xf;

	SetConsoleTextAttribute(GetStdHandle(STD_OUTPUT_HANDLE), color | (bgcolor << 4));
}

void OneCircleBattleEvent()
{
	skillChoice = 썾좰;
	battlecheck = 0;

	MonsterCreate();
	SkillCreate();

	monster1 = rand() % 4; // 0 ~ 3
	monster2 = rand() % 4; // 0 ~ 3

	while (monster1 == monster2)
	{
		monster2 = rand() % 4;
	}

	if (characterAgi >= monster[monster1].agi && characterAgi >= monster[monster2].agi) // 좙칮 왐얯 씱줮얯 瓚짔 : 1 > 2 > 씱
	{
		turn = 1;
		battlecheck = 7;
	}
	else if (characterAgi >= monster[monster1].agi && characterAgi < monster[monster2].agi) // 접쫔콼1 첇 씱줮얯 瓚쟞釜 2얙 씱줮얯 씽챹웒 콾 : 1 > 씱 > 2
	{
		turn = 2;
		battlecheck = 7;
	}
	else if (characterAgi >= monster[monster2].agi && characterAgi < monster[monster1].agi) // 접쫔콼2 쌰 씱줮얯 瓚쟞釜 1챸 씱줮얯 씽챹웒 콾 : 2 > 씱  > 1
	{
		turn = 3;
		battlecheck = 8;
	}
	else
	{
		turn = 3;
		battlecheck = 0;
	}
}

void OneCircleBattleScreen()
{
	system("cls");
	Sleep(1000);

	////////////////////////////////////////////////////// 줦쩠 (int) SkillChoice 턄절 狗
	SkillNameScreen();

	//////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////// 첔

	if (monster1 == 呼첇1 && monster[monster1].hp != 0)
	{
		MonkeyScreen();
	}
	else if (monster1 == 呼첇2 && monster[monster1].hp != 0)
	{
		MonkeyScreen();
	}
	else if (monster1 == 젃완쵔1 && monster[monster1].hp != 0)
	{
		WildboarScreen();
	}
	else if (monster1 == 젃완쵔2 && monster[monster1].hp != 0)
	{
		WildboarScreen();
	}
	else
	{
		EmptyScreen();
	}

	/////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////// 첔

	CharacterScreen();

	if (monster2 == 呼첇1 && monster[monster2].hp != 0)
	{
		MonkeyScreen();
	}
	else if (monster2 == 呼첇2 && monster[monster2].hp != 0)
	{
		MonkeyScreen();
	}
	else if (monster2 == 젃완쵔1 && monster[monster2].hp != 0)
	{
		WildboarScreen();
	}
	else if (monster2 == 젃완쵔2 && monster[monster2].hp != 0)
	{
		WildboarScreen();
	}
	else
	{
		EmptyScreen();
	}

	////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////// 첔

	BattleStatusScreen();

	////////////////////////////////////////////////////// 줦쩠 (int) battlecheck 턄절 狗

	BattleBottomScreen();
}


void SkillNameScreen()
{
	if (skillChoice == 쐑줱썾썧 && act == 1)
	{
		Skill0Screen();
	}
	else if (skillChoice == 쥠胄 && act == 1)
	{
		Skill1Screen();
	}
	else if (skillChoice == 얾콪썧 && act == 1)
	{
		Skill2Screen();
	}
	else if (skillChoice == 큊첲 && act == 1)
	{
		Skill3Screen();
	}
	else if (skillChoice == 좰첉첊쨨 && act == 1)
	{
		Skill4Screen();
	}
	else if (skillChoice == 쏛퀛츂 && act == 1)
	{
		Skill5Screen();
	}
	else if (skillChoice == 컫쵖썧 && act == 1)
	{
		Skill6Screen();
	}
	else
	{
		Skill7Screen();
	}
}

void BattleBottomScreen()
{
	if (battlecheck == 0)
	{
		BattleSkillScreen1();
	}
	else if (battlecheck == 1)
	{
		BattleSkillScreen2();
	}
	else if (battlecheck == 2)
	{
		BattleSkillScreen3();
	}
	else if (battlecheck == 3)
	{
		BattleSkillScreen4();
	}
	else if (battlecheck == 4)
	{
		BattleSkillScreen5();
	}
	else if (battlecheck == 5)
	{
		SelectMonster1Screen();
	}
	else if (battlecheck == 6)
	{
		SelectMonster2Screen();
	}
	else if (battlecheck == 7)
	{
		Monster1AttackScreen();
	}
	else if (battlecheck == 8)
	{
		Monster2AttackScreen();
	}
	else if (battlecheck == 9)
	{
		CharacterAttakScreen();
	}
	else if (battlecheck == 10)
	{
		CharacterErrorScreen();
	}
	else if (battlecheck == 11)
	{
		SelectMonster3Screen();
	}
	else if (battlecheck == 12)
	{
		SelectMonster4Screen();
	}
}

void BattleChoice()
{

	key = '0';
	key = _getch();

	if (key == (char)SPACE || key == (char)ENTER)
	{
		if (battlecheck == 0)
		{
			Skill = "쐑줱썾썧";
			skillChoice = 쐑줱썾썧;

			if (monster[monster1].hp > 0 && monster[monster2].hp > 0)
			{
				battlecheck = 5;
				OneCircleBattleScreen();
				BattleChoice();
			}
			else if (monster[monster1].hp > 0 && monster[monster2].hp <= 0)
			{
				battlecheck = 11;
				OneCircleBattleScreen();
				BattleChoice();
			}
			else if (monster[monster1].hp <= 0 && monster[monster2].hp > 0)
			{
				battlecheck = 12;
				OneCircleBattleScreen();
				BattleChoice();
			}
		}

		else if (battlecheck == 1)
		{
			Skill = characterSkill1;
			if (characterSkill1 == "쥠胄")
			{
				skillChoice = 쥠胄;
			}
			else
			{
				skillChoice = 얾콪썧;
			}


			if (monster[monster1].hp > 0 && monster[monster2].hp > 0)
			{
				battlecheck = 5;
				OneCircleBattleScreen();
				BattleChoice();
			}
			else if (monster[monster1].hp > 0 && monster[monster2].hp <= 0)
			{
				battlecheck = 11;
				OneCircleBattleScreen();
				BattleChoice();
			}
			else if (monster[monster1].hp <= 0 && monster[monster2].hp > 0)
			{
				battlecheck = 12;
				OneCircleBattleScreen();
				BattleChoice();
			}
		}

		else if (battlecheck == 2)
		{
			Skill = characterSkill2;
			if (characterSkill2 == "큊첲")
			{
				skillChoice = 큊첲家
			}
			else
			{
				skillChoice = 좰첉첊쨨;
			}


			if (monster[monster1].hp > 0 && monster[monster2].hp > 0)
			{
				battlecheck = 5;
				OneCircleBattleScreen();
				BattleChoice();
			}
			else if (monster[monster1].hp > 0 && monster[monster2].hp <= 0)
			{
				battlecheck = 11;
				OneCircleBattleScreen();
				BattleChoice();
			}
			else if (monster[monster1].hp <= 0 && monster[monster2].hp > 0)
			{
				battlecheck = 12;
				OneCircleBattleScreen();
				BattleChoice();
			}
		}

		else if (battlecheck == 3)
		{
			Skill = characterSkill3;
			if (characterSkill3 == "쏛퀛츂")
			{
				skillChoice = 쏛퀛츂;
			}
			else
			{
				skillChoice = 컫쵖썧;
			}

			if (monster[monster1].hp > 0 && monster[monster2].hp > 0)
			{
				battlecheck = 5;
				OneCircleBattleScreen();
				BattleChoice();
			}
			else if (monster[monster1].hp > 0 && monster[monster2].hp <= 0)
			{
				battlecheck = 11;
				OneCircleBattleScreen();
				BattleChoice();
			}
			else if (monster[monster1].hp <= 0 && monster[monster2].hp > 0)
			{
				battlecheck = 12;
				OneCircleBattleScreen();
				BattleChoice();
			}
		}

		else if (battlecheck == 4)
		{
			b_dungeoncheck = true;
			b_fieldcheck = false;
			Sleep(1400);
			auto fieldmusic = async(FieldMusic);
			FieldOneCircleScreen();
			FieldChoice();
		}

		else if (battlecheck == 5)
		{

			if (characterMp >= skill[skillChoice].mp)
			{
				monster[monster1].hp = monster[monster1].hp - skill[skillChoice].damage;
				if (monster[monster1].hp < 0)
				{
					monster[monster1].hp = 0;

				}
				act = 1;
				characterMp = characterMp - skill[skillChoice].mp;
				battlecheck = 9;
				OneCircleBattleScreen();
				BattleChoice();
			}
			else
			{
				battlecheck = 10;
				OneCircleBattleScreen();
				BattleChoice();
			}

		}
		else if (battlecheck == 6)
		{

			if (characterMp >= skill[skillChoice].mp)
			{
				monster[monster2].hp = monster[monster2].hp - skill[skillChoice].damage;
				if (monster[monster2].hp < 0)
				{
					monster[monster2].hp = 0;
				}
				act = 1;
				characterMp = characterMp - skill[skillChoice].mp;
				battlecheck = 9;
				OneCircleBattleScreen();
				BattleChoice();
			}
			else
			{
				battlecheck = 10;
				OneCircleBattleScreen();
				BattleChoice();
			}
		}
		else if (battlecheck == 7)
		{
			characterHp = characterHp - monster[monster1].atk;
			if (characterHp < 0)
			{
				characterHp = 0;
				//썞첍챷
			}
			else if (turn == 2)
			{
				battlecheck = 0; // 앁췽
				OneCircleBattleScreen();
				BattleChoice();
			}
			else
			{
				battlecheck = 8;
				OneCircleBattleScreen();
				BattleChoice();

			}
		}
		else if (battlecheck == 8)
		{
			characterHp = characterHp - monster[monster2].atk;
			if (characterHp < 0)
			{
				characterHp = 0;
				//썞첍챷
			}
			else if (turn == 2)
			{
				battlecheck = 8;
				OneCircleBattleScreen();
				BattleChoice();
			}
			else
			{
				battlecheck = 0; // 앁췽
				OneCircleBattleScreen();
				BattleChoice();
			}
		}
		else if (battlecheck == 9)
		{
			act = 0;

			if (monster[monster1].hp == 0 && monster[monster2].hp == 0)
			{
				// 쫙쟕
			}
			else if (turn == 1 || turn == 3)
			{
				battlecheck = 7;
				OneCircleBattleScreen();
				BattleChoice();
			}
			else if (turn == 2)
			{
				battlecheck = 8;
				OneCircleBattleScreen();
				BattleChoice();
			}
		}
		else if (battlecheck == 10)
		{
			battlecheck = 0;
			OneCircleBattleScreen();
			BattleChoice();
		}
		else if (battlecheck == 11)
		{

			if (characterMp >= skill[skillChoice].mp)
			{
				monster[monster1].hp = monster[monster1].hp - skill[skillChoice].damage;
				if (monster[monster1].hp < 0)
				{
					monster[monster1].hp = 0;

				}
				act = 1;
				characterMp = characterMp - skill[skillChoice].mp;
				battlecheck = 9;
				OneCircleBattleScreen();
				BattleChoice();
			}
			else
			{
				battlecheck = 10;
				OneCircleBattleScreen();
				BattleChoice();
			}
		}
		else if (battlecheck == 12)
		{

			if (characterMp >= skill[skillChoice].mp)
			{
				monster[monster2].hp = monster[monster2].hp - skill[skillChoice].damage;
				if (monster[monster2].hp < 0)
				{
					monster[monster2].hp = 0;
				}
				act = 1;
				characterMp = characterMp - skill[skillChoice].mp;
				battlecheck = 9;
				OneCircleBattleScreen();
				BattleChoice();
			}
			else
			{
				battlecheck = 10;
				OneCircleBattleScreen();
				BattleChoice();
			}
		}
		else
		{
			BattleChoice();
		}

	}

	else if (key == (char)UP || key == 'w' || key == 'W')
	{
		if (battlecheck == 1)
		{
			battlecheck = 0;
			OneCircleBattleScreen();
			BattleChoice();
		}
		else if (battlecheck == 2)
		{
			battlecheck = 1;
			OneCircleBattleScreen();
			BattleChoice();
		}
		else if (battlecheck == 3)
		{
			battlecheck = 2;
			OneCircleBattleScreen();
			BattleChoice();
		}
		else if (battlecheck == 4)
		{
			if (characterSkill3 == "" && characterSkill2 == "")
			{
				battlecheck = 1;
				OneCircleBattleScreen();
				BattleChoice();
			}
			else if (characterSkill3 == "" && characterSkill2 != "")
			{
				battlecheck = 2;
				OneCircleBattleScreen();
				BattleChoice();
			}
			else
			{
				battlecheck = 3;
				OneCircleBattleScreen();
				BattleChoice();
			}
		}
		else if (battlecheck == 6)
		{
			battlecheck = 5;
			OneCircleBattleScreen();
			BattleChoice();
		}
		else if (battlecheck == 0)
		{
			battlecheck = 0;
			OneCircleBattleScreen();
			BattleChoice();
		}
		else if (battlecheck == 5)
		{
			battlecheck = 5;
			OneCircleBattleScreen();
			BattleChoice();
		}
		else
		{
			BattleChoice();
		}

	}

	else if (key == (char)DOWN || key == 's' || key == 'S')
	{
		if (battlecheck == 0)
		{
			battlecheck = 1;
			OneCircleBattleScreen();
			BattleChoice();
		}
		else if (battlecheck == 1)
		{
			if (characterSkill2 != "")
			{
				battlecheck = 2;
				OneCircleBattleScreen();
				BattleChoice();
			}
			else
			{
				battlecheck = 4;
				OneCircleBattleScreen();
				BattleChoice();
			}
		}
		else if (battlecheck == 2)
		{
			if (characterSkill3 != "")
			{
				battlecheck = 3;
				OneCircleBattleScreen();
				BattleChoice();
			}
			else
			{
				battlecheck = 4;
				OneCircleBattleScreen();
				BattleChoice();
			}
		}
		else if (battlecheck == 3)
		{
			battlecheck = 4;
			OneCircleBattleScreen();
			BattleChoice();
		}
		else if (battlecheck == 5)
		{
			battlecheck = 6;
			OneCircleBattleScreen();
			BattleChoice();
		}
		else if (battlecheck == 4)
		{
			battlecheck = 4;
			OneCircleBattleScreen();
			BattleChoice();
		}
		else if (battlecheck == 6)
		{
			battlecheck = 6;
			OneCircleBattleScreen();
			BattleChoice();
		}
		else
		{
			OneCircleBattleScreen();
			BattleChoice();
		}
	}
}


void MonsterCreate()
{

	//////////////////////////////////////////////////

	monster[呼첇1].name = "呼첇";

	monster[呼첇1].level = rand() % ((characterLevel + 2) - (characterLevel - 6) + 1) + (characterLevel - 6);
	while (monster[呼첇1].level < 1)
	{
		monster[呼첇1].level = rand() % ((characterLevel + 2) - (characterLevel)+1) + (characterLevel - 6);
	}

	monster[呼첇1].exp = monster[呼첇1].level * 550;
	monster[呼첇1].hp = monster[呼첇1].level * 750;
	monster[呼첇1].atk = (monster[呼첇1].level * 100) + (rand() % 10 + 1);
	monster[呼첇1].agi = rand() % 7 + 4;
	monster[呼첇1].money = rand() % 500 + 3000;

	//////////////////////////////////////////////////

	monster[呼첇2].name = "呼첇";

	monster[呼첇2].level = rand() % ((characterLevel + 2) - (characterLevel - 6) + 1) + (characterLevel - 6);
	while (monster[呼첇2].level < 1)
	{
		monster[呼첇2].level = rand() % ((characterLevel + 2) - (characterLevel - 6) + 1) + (characterLevel - 6);
	}

	monster[呼첇2].exp = monster[呼첇2].level * 750;
	monster[呼첇2].hp = monster[呼첇2].level * 750;
	monster[呼첇2].atk = (monster[呼첇2].level * 100) + (rand() % 10 + 1);
	monster[呼첇2].agi = rand() % 7 + 4;
	monster[呼첇2].money = rand() % 500 + 3000;

	//////////////////////////////////////////////////

	monster[젃완쵔1].name = "젃완쵔";
	monster[젃완쵔1].level = rand() % ((characterLevel + 2) - (characterLevel - 6) + 1) + (characterLevel - 6);
	while (monster[젃완쵔1].level < 1)
	{
		monster[젃완쵔1].level = rand() % ((characterLevel + 2) - (characterLevel - 6) + 1) + (characterLevel - 6);
	}

	monster[젃완쵔1].exp = monster[젃완쵔1].level * 800;
	monster[젃완쵔1].hp = monster[젃완쵔1].level * 770;
	monster[젃완쵔1].atk = (monster[젃완쵔1].level * 120) + (rand() % 10 + 1);
	monster[젃완쵔1].agi = rand() % 7 + 4;
	monster[젃완쵔1].money = rand() % 500 + 3500;

	//////////////////////////////////////////////////

	monster[젃완쵔2].name = "젃완쵔";
	monster[젃완쵔2].level = rand() % ((characterLevel + 2) - (characterLevel - 6) + 1) + (characterLevel - 6);
	while (monster[젃완쵔2].level < 1)
	{
		monster[젃완쵔2].level = rand() % ((characterLevel + 2) - (characterLevel - 6) + 1) + (characterLevel - 6);
	}

	monster[젃완쵔2].exp = monster[젃완쵔2].level * 800;
	monster[젃완쵔2].hp = monster[젃완쵔2].level * 770;
	monster[젃완쵔2].atk = (monster[젃완쵔2].level * 120) + (rand() % 10 + 1);
	monster[젃완쵔2].agi = rand() % 7 + 4;
	monster[젃완쵔2].money = rand() % 500 + 3500;

	//////////////////////////////////////////////////

	monster[옸立].name = "옸";
	monster[옸立].level = rand() % ((characterLevel + 2) - (characterLevel - 5) + 1) + (characterLevel);

	monster[옸立].exp = monster[옸立].level * 800;
	monster[옸立].hp = monster[옸立].level * 770;
	monster[옸立].atk = (monster[옸立].level * 142) + (rand() % 10 + 1);
	monster[옸立].agi = rand() % 7 + 4;
	monster[옸立].money = rand() % 500 + 4500;

	//////////////////////////////////////////////////

	monster[옸笠].name = "옸";
	monster[옸笠].level = rand() % ((characterLevel + 2) - (characterLevel - 5) + 1) + (characterLevel);
	monster[옸笠].exp = monster[옸笠].level * 800;
	monster[옸笠].hp = monster[옸笠].level * 770;
	monster[옸笠].atk = (monster[옸笠].level * 142) + (rand() % 10 + 1);
	monster[옸笠].agi = rand() % 7 + 4;
	monster[옸笠].money = rand() % 500 + 4500;

	//////////////////////////////////////////////////

	monster[좤쵂1].name = "좤쵂";
	monster[좤쵂1].level = rand() % ((characterLevel + 2) - (characterLevel - 5) + 1) + (characterLevel);
	monster[좤쵂1].exp = monster[좤쵂1].level * 800;
	monster[좤쵂1].hp = monster[좤쵂1].level * 770;
	monster[좤쵂1].atk = (monster[좤쵂1].level * 142) + (rand() % 10 + 1);
	monster[좤쵂1].agi = rand() % 7 + 4;
	monster[좤쵂1].money = rand() % 500 + 4000;

	//////////////////////////////////////////////////

	monster[좤쵂2].name = "좤쵂";
	monster[좤쵂2].level = rand() % ((characterLevel + 2) - (characterLevel - 5) + 1) + (characterLevel);
	monster[좤쵂2].exp = monster[좤쵂2].level * 800;
	monster[좤쵂2].hp = monster[좤쵂2].level * 770;
	monster[좤쵂2].atk = (monster[좤쵂2].level * 142) + (rand() % 10 + 1);
	monster[좤쵂2].agi = rand() % 7 + 4;
	monster[좤쵂2].money = rand() % 500 + 4000;

	//////////////////////////////////////////////////

	monster[촋퀛첉1].name = "촋퀛첉";
	monster[촋퀛첉1].level = rand() % ((characterLevel + 2) - (characterLevel - 5) + 1) + (characterLevel);
	monster[촋퀛첉1].exp = monster[촋퀛첉1].level * 800;
	monster[촋퀛첉1].hp = monster[촋퀛첉1].level * 770;
	monster[촋퀛첉1].atk = (monster[촋퀛첉1].level * 142) + (rand() % 10 + 1);
	monster[촋퀛첉1].agi = rand() % 7 + 4;
	monster[촋퀛첉1].money = rand() % 500 + 5000;

	//////////////////////////////////////////////////

	monster[촋퀛첉2].name = "촋퀛첉";
	monster[촋퀛첉2].level = rand() % ((characterLevel + 2) - (characterLevel - 5) + 1) + (characterLevel);
	monster[촋퀛첉2].exp = monster[촋퀛첉2].level * 800;
	monster[촋퀛첉2].hp = monster[촋퀛첉2].level * 770;
	monster[촋퀛첉2].atk = (monster[촋퀛첉2].level * 142) + (rand() % 10 + 1);
	monster[촋퀛첉2].agi = rand() % 7 + 4;
	monster[촋퀛첉2].money = rand() % 500 + 5000;

	//////////////////////////////////////////////////

	monster[茅첉1].name = "茅첉";
	monster[茅첉1].level = rand() % ((characterLevel + 2) - (characterLevel - 5) + 1) + (characterLevel);
	monster[茅첉1].exp = monster[茅첉1].level * 800;

void SkillCreate()
{

	skill[쐑줱썾썧].name = "쐑줱썾썧";
	skill[쐑줱썾썧].damage = characterAtk;
	skill[쐑줱썾썧].mp = 0;

	skill[쥠胄묗.name = "쥠胄";
	skill[쥠胄묗.damage = (characterAtk * 2) + rand() % 50;
	skill[쥠胄묗.mp = 300;

	skill[얾콪썧].name = "얾콪썧";
	skill[얾콪썧].damage = (characterAtk * 3) + rand() % 50;
	skill[얾콪썧].mp = 200;

	skill[큊첲姦.name = "큊첲";
	skill[큊첲姦.damage = (characterAtk * 10) + rand() % 100;
	skill[큊첲姦.mp = 2500;

	skill[좰첉첊쨨].name = "좰첉첊쨨";
	skill[좰첉첊쨨].damage = (characterAtk * 11) + rand() % 100;
	skill[좰첉첊쨨].mp = 2000;

	skill[쏛퀛츂].name = "쏛퀛츂";
	skill[쏛퀛츂].damage = (characterAtk * 50) + rand() % 100;
	skill[쏛퀛츂].mp = 8200;

	skill[컫쵖썧].name = "컫쵖썧";
	skill[컫쵖썧].damage = (characterAtk * 40) + rand() % 100;
	skill[컫쵖썧].mp = 7500;

}
